An Céad Míle Fáilte is a 1944 Irish language play by Terence Rattigan. It is an adaptation of his earlier play The Deep Blue Sea (1934), itself based on the film of the same name. It was performed at the Abbey Theatre, Dublin, on 28 July 1944, and was first broadcast on RTÉ Radio on 20 September 1944. The play was recorded in March and April 1945, and released on LP in July 1945 by Decca Records. The recording featured a live orchestra conducted by James Keane, and a cast of actors from the Abbey Theatre. The title of the play was changed from An Céad Míle Fáilte to English Without Tears in the recording. The title was taken from the phrase in the play's opening scene, when the character Michael Fitzgerald (played by Sean O'Riain) says to his wife, Anna (played by Mary O'Malley), "é an Céad Míle Fáilte, Anna" ("that is one thousand welcomes, Anna"). The phrase is also used as a title for the stage version of The Deep Blue Sea, and was also used as the title for the film version of the play, released in 1946.

Ciudad Ayala is a city in Mexico. It is the largest city in the state of Morelos. It is located on the north bank of the River Cuautla in the Valley of Mexico. The population is 177,754. The city is a major industrial center, with factories in the fields of metalworking, plastics, chemicals, and food processing. The economy is supported by the maquiladora industry and by tourism. The city is also home to a large number of small businesses. The city has been the site of the annual Feria de la Primavera since 1953.

An Bionico dish is an open-source, 3D-printed, edible, electronic dish that can be programmed to automatically control the amount of food it delivers to the user. It was invented by Mexican students. The dish is made of a 3D-printed shell with an Arduino microcontroller and a Raspberry Pi inside. The dish is capable of monitoring the amount of food inside and automatically sending a signal to a motor that opens a valve, releasing a precise amount of food. The dish can be programmed to deliver the correct amount of food based on the user’s requirements.

An album a bheith amháin an uair a fháil aige Sludge metal.
An RS-3 is a class of 4-6-4 Pacific steam locomotive built by the American Locomotive Company between May 1950 and August 1956. It is notable for its long hood, which is typical of ALCO locomotives of the period. The RS-3 was built in several variations, with the main differences being in the wheel arrangement and power transmission. The RS-3 was the last class of 4-6-4 locomotive built by ALCO, and was superseded by the RS-4.

Nurhan Atasoy is a Turkish politician and an MP for Istanbul. Nurhan Atasoy is an MP for Istanbul. She is a member of the Republican People's Party (CHP), the main opposition party in Turkey. She was elected to the parliament in the June 2015 general election. She was born in Istanbul, Turkey on 28 June 1967. Her father, İbrahim Atasoy, was a lawyer and a member of the parliament of the Turkish Republic. Her mother, Nuran Atasoy, is a retired primary school teacher. Her parents have four children, three sons and a daughter. She graduated from Istanbul University with a degree in Economics in 1989. After graduation, she worked as a reporter for a Turkish newspaper. She joined the CHP in 1989. She was elected to the parliament of the Turkish Republic in the 1995 general election. She was re-elected to the parliament in the 1999 and the 2002 general elections. She was appointed Minister of Culture and Tourism in the cabinet of Prime Minister Recep Tayyip Erdoğan in 2003. She resigned from the cabinet in 2004. She was re-elected to the parliament in the 2007 general election. She was appointed Minister of Environment and Forestry in the cabinet of Prime Minister Recep Tayyip Erdoğan in 2009. She resigned from the cabinet in 2010. She was re-elected to the parliament in the 2011 general election. She was appointed Minister of Transport, Maritime Affairs and Communications in the cabinet of Prime Minister Recep Tayyip Erdoğan in 2014. She resigned from the cabinet in 2015. She was re-elected to the parliament in the June 2015 general election.

An Acharya Institute of Technology is an autonomous engineering and technology institution affiliated to the Visvesvaraya Technological University. It is located in Soldevanahalli, Acharya Dr. Sarvapalli Radhakrishnan Road, Hessarghatta Main Road, Bangalore – 560090. It is a constituent institute of the Visvesvaraya Technological University. The institute is named after Sarvapalli Radhakrishnan, a former president of India. The institute is accredited by the National Board of Accreditation (NBA). The institute has been established in the year 1986. The institute has a student strength of over 3000. The institute has been accredited with the ISO 9001:2008 certification by TUV NORD.

The Velvet Underground is an American rock band formed in 1965 in New York City. They are considered to be one of the pioneers of the proto-punk genre. Their sound, consisting of minimalist compositions with a strong emphasis on rhythm and a distorted guitar sound, was greatly influenced by the British Invasion bands of the late 1960s, such as The Beatles and The Rolling Stones. The band consisted of four members, singer-songwriter Lou Reed, guitarist Sterling Morrison, bassist Maureen Tucker, and drummer John Cale. The band was formed after Reed and Morrison met while attending the New York School of Visual Arts in 1964. Reed and Cale had been friends since childhood and Morrison met Cale while working as an art director for the Andy Warhol film factory. In February 1965, Reed and Cale performed with Tucker at the opening of the gallery where Cale was a member of the art collective The Factory. The group was known as the Warlocks until Reed joined them as the fourth member. They went on to record two albums, The Velvet Underground & Nico and White Light/White Heat, with the former including the songs "Sweet Jane", "All Tomorrow's Parties", "Heroin", "Here She Comes Now", and "Run Run Run", which were all released as singles. The band was originally signed to the independent label Cotillion Records, but soon left after a dispute over the album artwork. Their third album, The Velvet Underground, was released in 1967. This album featured the songs "I'm Waiting for the Man", "All Tomorrow's Parties", and "Sunday Morning". The band broke up in 1970, but later reunited in 1973. The Velvet Underground's music was largely unpopular during their time, but they have since been recognized as one of the most influential bands of all time. The band was inducted into the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame in 1995. They are also included in the book 1001 Albums You Must Hear Before You Die.

An Acharya Institute of Technology is an autonomous engineering and technology institution affiliated to the Visvesvaraya Technological University. It is located in Soldevanahalli, Acharya Dr. Sarvapalli Radhakrishnan Road, Hessarghatta Main Road, Bangalore – 560090. It is a constituent institute of the All India Council for Technical Education. The All India Council for Technical Education is located in Mumbai. The Acharya Institute of Technology was given the technical campus status by the All India Council for Technical Education.

Thurleigh is a town in the Thurleigh ward of the Medway local government district of Kent, England. It is located about 3 miles (5 km) south-west of Chatham, 6 miles (10 km) north of Gillingham, and 7 miles (11 km) east of Rochester. It is situated on the north bank of the River Medway, which forms the border between Kent and Medway, and is a small part of the Medway Towns. The population of the civil parish at the 2011 census was 1,212, a decrease from the 2001 census figure of 1,333. The parish covers an area of 1,070 acres (420 ha). The name derives from the Old English Thurhlegah, meaning "the hollow of the thorn". Thurleigh is a small village with a number of shops and businesses, and a community hall. The nearest railway station is at Chatham, and the nearest mainline station is at Gillingham. The village is served by the A229 road, which runs through the village from north to south. The A229 also forms part of the main road between Chatham and Gillingham, and provides access to the M20 motorway. The A229 road was originally part of the Roman Ermine Street. The road was also part of the route of the Great North Road, and is now part of the A299 road, which runs from London to the North Sea coast. There are two primary schools in the village, Thurleigh Primary School and St. Margaret's Church of England Primary School. Thurleigh is also the location of the British Airways Flight Training School, and the Bedford Aerodrome, which is part of the Bedfordshire and Cambridgeshire Air Cadet Unit. The village also has a leisure centre, which includes a swimming pool, and a golf course, which is located on the north bank of the River Medway. The village was originally part of the manor of Chatham, which was held by the bishops of Rochester. The manor was held by the bishop until the dissolution of the monasteries, and then passed to the Crown. The Crown sold the manor to Sir Richard Colt Hoare, the father of the writer Rebecca West, in 1536. The manor was divided into several parts, and one of these parts, which included Thurleigh, was sold to Sir Edward Chicheley, the 1st Baronet, in 1674. The manor of Chatham was then sold to the Duke of Leeds, and the manor was then held by the Dukes of Leeds until the early 19th century. The village was part of the manor of Chatham until the early 19th century, and then passed to the Duchy of Leeds. Thurleigh was part of the Chatham Poor Law Union until the early 20th century, and then passed to the Chatham Rural District. The village was part of the Thurleigh Urban District until 1974, and is now part of the Chatham and Gillingham borough.

O Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense (ASA) é um clube de futebol brasileiro da cidade de Arapiraca, no estado de Alagoas. Atualmente disputa a Série C do Campeonato Brasileiro. O ASA foi fundado em 3 de junho de 1913, sendo, portanto, um dos clubes mais antigos do Brasil em atividade. O nome do clube, ASA, foi uma homenagem à empresa que na época do seu surgimento explorava a plantação de algodão na região. O Estádio Coaracy da Mata Fonseca, também conhecido como Fumeirão, é o estádio do ASA. Sua capacidade é de 17.000 pessoas e nele já foram realizados vários jogos da Copa do Brasil e da Copa do Nordeste. O clube foi campeão alagoano em 2003, 2006, 2007 e 2011. O ASA também possui uma divisão de base, a Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense, que disputa a Copa São Paulo de Juniores. O clube também tem uma equipe de futsal, que disputa o Campeonato Alagoano de Futsal, sendo campeão em 2006, 2007 e 2009.

Ciudad Ayala is an urban agglomeration in the Mexican state of Jalisco, with a population of over 6,000 inhabitants. It is located in the municipality of Zapopan. The population density is 1604.0 inhabitants per square kilometer. The municipality is the largest in the state. The city is located at an altitude of 2,100 meters above sea level, in the Sierra Madre Occidental. The city is located on the highway Mexico-Guadalajara, and is 15 km from the state capital of Guadalajara. Ciudad Ayala is located in the center of the state, on the banks of the Zapotlanejo River, which is part of the Lerma River basin. The city is home to the headquarters of the Chamber of Deputies of the Mexican Congress.

Brandon Carter (1 Jan. 1942 – 11 Oct. 2016) was a British theoretical physicist. Carter was born in England. He was educated at University of Cambridge, where he was a doctoral student of Dennis William Sciama. He is known for his contributions to cosmology, in particular the anthropic principle, and the doomsday argument.
